        || /1207|6310|6590|3gso|4thp|50[1-6]i|770s|802s|a wa|abac|ac(er|oo|s\-)|ai(ko|rn)|al(av|ca|co)|amoi|an(ex|ny|yw)|aptu|ar(ch|go)|as(te|us)|attw|au(di|\-m|r |s )|avan|be(ck|ll|nq)|bi(lb|rd)|bl(ac|az)|br(e|v)w|bumb|bw\-(n|u)|c55\/|capi|ccwa|cdm\-|cell|chtm|cldc|cmd\-|co(mp|nd)|craw|da(it|ll|ng)|dbte|dc\-s|devi|dica|dmob|do(c|p)o|ds(12|\-d)|el(49|ai)|em(l2|ul)|er(ic|k0)|esl8|ez([4-7]0|os|wa|ze)|fetc|fly(\-|_)|g1 u|g560|gene|gf\-5|g\-mo|go(\.w|od)|gr(ad|un)|haie|hcit|hd\-(m|p|t)|hei\-|hi(pt|ta)|hp( i|ip)|hs\-c|ht(c(\-| |_|a|g|p|s|t)|tp)|hu(aw|tc)|i\-(20|go|ma)|i230|iac( |\-|\/)|ibro|idea|ig01|ikom|im1k|inno|ipaq|iris|ja(t|v)a|jbro|jemu|jigs|kddi|keji|kgt( |\/)|klon|kpt |kwc\-|kyo(c|k)|le(no|xi)|lg( g|\/(k|l|u)|50|54|\-[a-w])|libw|lynx|m1\-w|m3ga|m50\/|ma(te|ui|xo)|mc(01|21|ca)|m\-cr|me(rc|ri)|mi(o8|oa|ts)|mmef|mo(01|02|bi|de|do|t(\-| |o|v)|zz)|mt(50|p1|v )|mwbp|mywa|n10[0-2]|n20[2-3]|n30(0|2)|n50(0|2|5)|n7(0(0|1)|10)|ne((c|m)\-|on|tf|wf|wg|wt)|nok(6|i)|nzph|o2im|op(ti|wv)|oran|owg1|p800|pan(a|d|t)|pdxg|pg(13|\-([1-8]|c))|phil|pire|pl(ay|uc)|pn\-2|po(ck|rt|se)|prox|psio|pt\-g|qa\-a|qc(07|12|21|32|60|\-[2-7]|i\-)|qtek|r380|r600|raks|rim9|ro(ve|zo)|s55\/|sa(ge|ma|mm|ms|ny|va)|sc(01|h\-|oo|p\-)|sdk\/|se(c(\-|0|1)|47|mc|nd|ri)|sgh\-|shar|sie(\-|m)|sk\-0|sl(45|id)|sm(al|ar|b3|it|t5)|so(ft|ny)|sp(01|h\-|v\-|v )|sy(01|mb)|t2(18|50)|t6(00|10|18)|ta(gt|lk)|tcl\-|tdg\-|tel(i|m)|tim\-|t\-mo|to(pl|sh)|ts(70|m\-|m3|m5)|tx\-9|up(\.b|g1|si)|utst|v400|v750|veri|vi(rg|te)|vk(40|5[0-3]|\-v)|vm40|voda|vulc|vx(52|53|60|61|70|80|81|83|85|98)|w3c(\-| )|webc|whit|wi(g |nc|nw)|wmlb|wonu|x700|yas\-|your|zeto|zte\-/i.test(navigator.userAgent.substr(0,4)));
    
        adition.onLoad = function(callback) {
        adition.onLoadCallbacks.push(callback);
        return adition;
    };
    const _onPostRenderCallbacks = [];
    adition.onPostRender = function(callback) {
        _onPostRenderCallbacks.push(callback);
        return adition;
    };
    const _onNoBannerCallbacks = [];
    adition.onNoBanner = function(callback) {
        _onNoBannerCallbacks.push(callback);
        return adition;
    };
    const _onFinishLoadingCallbacks = [];
    adition.onFinishLoading = function(callback) {
        _onFinishLoadingCallbacks.push(callback);
        return adition;
    };
    adition.srq.push(function(api) {
        api.events
            .onPostRender(function(renderSlotElement, bannerDescriptionApi, renderControlApi) {
                _onPostRenderCallbacks.forEach(function(callback) {
                    callback.call(adition, renderSlotElement, bannerDescriptionApi, renderControlApi);
                });
            })
            .onNoBanner(function(renderSlotElement, bannerDescriptionApi, renderControlApi) {
                _onNoBannerCallbacks.forEach(function(callback) {
                    callback.call(adition, renderSlotElement, bannerDescriptionApi, renderControlApi);
                });
            })
            .onFinishLoading(function(renderSlotElement, bannerDescriptionApi, renderControlApi) {
                _onFinishLoadingCallbacks.forEach(function(callback) {
                    callback.call(adition, renderSlotElement, bannerDescriptionApi, renderControlApi);
                });
            });
    });
    
    adition.isBannerAvailable = function(banner) {
        banner = banner.replace(/[\s\(\)]/g, '');
        const bannerCfg = adition.bannerMappings[banner] || [];
        const mappedBanner = bannerCfg[adition.isMobile ? 'mobile' : 'desktop'] || banner;

        if (mappedBanner === false) {
            return false; //disabled for device by mapping config
        }

        for (var b in adition.adSlots) {
            const slotConf = adition.adSlots[b];
            const slotName = slotConf.banner.replace(/[\s\(\)]/g, '');
            if (slotName === mappedBanner) {
                
                //spunq-cms conf has the winning hand
                if (slotConf[adition.displayContext] === false) {
                    return false;
                }

                //mapping config may override for disabling a banner
                if (bannerCfg.channel === false && adition.displayContext === 'channel') {
                    return false;
                }
                if (bannerCfg.article === false && adition.displayContext === 'article') {
                    return false;
                }

                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    };
    adition.getRenderId = function(banner) {
        banner = banner.replace(/[\s\(\)]/g, '');

        if (!adition.isBannerAvailable(banner)) {
            return null;
        }

        if (adition.bannerMappings[banner]) {
            const bannerCfg = adition.bannerMappings[banner];
            const mappedBanner = bannerCfg[adition.isMobile ? 'mobile' : 'desktop'];
            if (mappedBanner !== undefined && mappedBanner !== true) {
                return mappedBanner; //mapped name
            }
        }
        return banner;
    };
    
    var _availableBanners = [];
    adition.getAvailableBanners = function(callback) {
        if (!callback && _availableBanners.length > 0) {
            return _availableBanners;
        }
        const _banners = [];
        adition.adSlots.forEach(function(adSlot) {
            if (adition.isBannerAvailable(adSlot.banner)) {
                if (!callback || callback.call(adSlot, adition.bannerMappings[adSlot.banner]) === true) {
                    _banners.push(adSlot.banner);
                }
            }
        });
        return _availableBanners = _banners;
    };
    adition.getVisibleBanners = function(callback) {
        const _visibles = [];
        adition.getAvailableBanners(callback).forEach(function(banner) {
            const bannerId = adition.getRenderId(banner);
            const bannerEl = document.getElementById(bannerId);
            if (bannerEl && bannerEl.dataset.inViewPort === "yes") {
                _visibles.push(bannerId);
            }
        });
        return _visibles;
    };
    adition.isBannerVisible = function(banner) {
        return adition.getVisibleBanners().indexOf(adition.getRenderId(banner)) > -1;
    };
    adition.hasLazyLoad = function(banner) {
        // global setting overrules
        if (adition.disableLazyLoad) {
            return false;
        }
        banner = adition.getRenderId(banner);
        return (!adition.bannerMappings[banner] || adition.bannerMappings[banner].lazyload !== false);
    };
    adition.renderSlot = function(banner, lazyLoad) {
        const bannerEl = document.getElementById(banner);
        const bannerId = adition.getRenderId(banner);

        if (!bannerId) {
                    return false;
        }

        bannerEl.id = bannerId;
        bannerEl.dataset.renderName = banner;

        adition.srq.push(function(api) {
            api.renderSlot(bannerId);
        });

        if (adition.hasLazyLoad(banner) !== true) {
            bannerEl.dataset.adSlotLoaded = "yes";
            _initialRenderSlots.push(bannerId);
        }
        _iObserver.observe(bannerEl);

        return bannerEl;
    };
    adition.queueLoad = function() {
                adition.srq.push(
            function(api) {
                // console.log('aditionSetup.tpl: starting rendering. ');
                for (var cb in adition.onLoadCallbacks) {
                    adition.onLoadCallbacks[cb].call(adition, api);
                }
                adition.requestBanners(_initialRenderSlots);
                adition.loaded = true;
            }
        );
    };

    var _requestingBanners = null;
    adition.requestBanners = function(bannerIds) {
        if (!bannerIds || bannerIds.length < 1) return;
        if (_requestingBanners !== null) { //already a request in process, go easy on adition
            setTimeout(function() {
                adition.requestBanners(bannerIds);
            }, 160);
            return;
        }
        _requestingBanners = bannerIds;
        adition.srq.push(function(api) {
                        api
                .load(bannerIds)
                .completeRendering(bannerIds);
        });
    };
    adition
        .onPostRender(function() {
            _requestingBanners = null;
        })
        .onNoBanner(function() {
            _requestingBanners = null;
        })
        .onFinishLoading(function() {
            _requestingBanners = null;
        });

    adition.consentSubmitted = false;
    adition.consentSubmit = function(iabString, force) {
        if (adition.consentSubmitted && !force) return;
        adition.srq.push(
            function(api) {
                api.consentService
                    .setGdprConsent(iabString)
                    .setGdpr(1)
                    .setGdprPd(1);
            }
        );
        adition.consentSubmitted = true;
    };


    adition.srq.push(function(api) {

        // Configure modules ...
        // api.modules.setLoadingTimeout(2000);

        var yieldLab;
            yieldLab = api.modules.configureModule('yieldlab');
    
        for (var adSlot in adition.adSlots) {
            const bannerConf = adition.adSlots[adSlot];
            const renderId = adition.getRenderId(bannerConf.banner);

            if (!renderId) {
                            continue;
            }
                    if (renderId.match(/^video/i)) {
                            continue;
            }
        
            const yieldConf = bannerConf.yieldLab;
            if (yieldLab && typeof yieldConf != undefined) {
                for (var yk in yieldConf) {
                    yieldLab.mapContentunit(
                        bannerConf.id, 
                        yieldConf[yk].yieldId, 
                        yieldConf[yk].yieldFormat
                    );
                }
            }

            
            api.configureRenderSlot(renderId).setContentunitId(parseInt(bannerConf.id));
        }
        yieldLab.enable();

        api.registerAdfarm("ad1.adfarm1.adition.com");
        api.setProfile('userLang', navigator.language || navigator.userLanguage);
            api.setProfile('adPageName', 'frontpage');
            api.setProfile('adStory', '');
            api.setProfile('adReload', 'false');
            api.setProfile('warningType_kaernten', 'storm');
            api.setProfile('warningIntensity_kaernten', '1');
            api.setProfile('warningType_tirol', 'storm');
            api.setProfile('warningIntensity_tirol', '1');
            api.setProfile('warningType_burgenland', 'storm');
            api.setProfile('warningIntensity_burgenland', '1');
            api.setProfile('warningType_niederoesterreich', 'storm');
            api.setProfile('warningIntensity_niederoesterreich', '1');
            api.setProfile('warningType_steiermark', 'storm');
            api.setProfile('warningIntensity_steiermark', '1');
           
    });
    
    window.addEventListener("load", function(e) {
        if (adition.loaded || typeof adition === 'undefined') {
            return;
        }
        if (typeof __tcfapi === 'undefined') {              adition.queueLoad();
        }
    });

    window.addEventListener("tcfConsentLoaded", function(e) {
        adition.consentSubmit(e.tcString);
        adition.queueLoad();
    });

})();

     <script>
      $(function () {

            'use strict';

            $('.navbar [data-toggle="offcanvas"]').on('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                                $('body').toggleClass('offCanvas');
                $('.offcanvas-collapse').scrollTop(0).toggleClass('open');
            });

            $('.offcanvas-collapse').on('click', function(e) {
                if (e.target === this) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                                        $('body').toggleClass('offCanvas');
                    $('.offcanvas-collapse').toggleClass('open');
                    $('.offcanvas-collapse .dropdownToggle').removeClass('open');
                    $('.offCanvasSubNav.open').removeClass('open');
                }
            });

            $('.offcanvas-collapse .dropdownToggle').on('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                $(this).toggleClass('open');
                $(this).next('[aria-labelledby="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').toggleClass('open');
            });

        });
     </script>

       (function() {
        $(document).ready(function() {
            
            var slider = null;
            function loadConsole442(){
                slider = $('.console[data-id="442"] .consoleStories').lightSlider({
                    gallery:true,
                    autoWidth:false,
                    item:1,
                    loop:true,
                    slideMove:1,
                    slideMargin:0,
                    enableDrag:true,
                    enableTouch:true,
                    controls:false,
                    currentPagerPosition: 'left',
                                            thumbItem:5,
                        pager:true,
                                                            responsive : [
                        {
                            breakpoint:900,
                            settings: {
                                thumbItem:3,
                            }
                        },
                        {
                            breakpoint:620,
                            settings: {
                                thumbItem:2,
                            }
                        }
                    ],
                    onBeforeSlide: function() {
                        iom.c(oewa_data,1);                                        
                    },
                    onAfterSlide: function(el) {
                        $('#consoleCounter442').html(el.getCurrentSlideCount() + '/22');    
                        el.getCurrentSlideCount();                       
                    },

                    onSliderLoad: function(){
                        handleThumbnails442();                        window.setTimeout(initNav442, 50);
                    }
                });
            }
            var stories442 = new Array();
                            stories442[0] = 'Mord in Salzburg: Mann ersticht seine Frau';
                            stories442[1] = 'Corona-Positive verließen aus Langeweile Quarantäne';
                            stories442[2] = 'Nachrichten-Sperre: Sorge um FPÖ-Chef ';
                            stories442[3] = '';
                            stories442[4] = 'Surf-Star (22) von Blitz getroffen - tot';
                            stories442[5] = 'Paar bricht in Kino ein und hat Sex vor der Leinwand';
                            stories442[6] = 'AMS-Skandal: Keine Hilfe wegen E-Mail-Irrläufer';
                            stories442[7] = '';

                            stories442[11] = '';

                            stories442[13] = 'Impfchaos: Stadt Wien gibt Doppeltermine zu';
                            stories442[14] = 'Corona: Südafrika verkauft seine Impfdosen an Nachbarn ';

            function findElement442(){

                if($('.console[data-id="442"] .container.headline').is(":visible")){
                    loadConsole442();
                    return;
                }
                window.setTimeout(findElement442, 1000);
            }
            findElement442();

                            window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
                    setTimeout(handleThumbnails442, 200);
                });
                
                var oe24SetButtonHeight442 = setInterval(setButtonSize442, 500);
               
                function setButtonSize442(){
                    var height = $('.console[data-id="442"] .lSPager>li img').innerHeight();
                    if(height>0) {
                        $('.console[data-id="442"] .pagerContainer button').height(height+'px');
                        clearInterval(oe24SetButtonHeight442);
                    }
                }
                
                function handleThumbnails442(){
                    $('.console[data-id="442"] ul.lSPager li').each(function(i){
                        var id = (i+1);
                        // counter
                        var $divCounter = $("<div>", {"class": "storyCounter"});
                        $divCounter.html(id);

                        $(this).append($divCounter);

                        // text
                        var $divText = $("<div>", {"class": "storyCaption"});
                        var $nodeMarker = $("<span>", {"class": "storyMarker"});
                        var $nodeText = $("<span>", {"class": "title"});
                        $nodeText.html(stories442[i]);

                        $divText.append($nodeMarker);
                        $divText.append($nodeText);

                        $(this).append($divText);
                    });

                    // set height - importend for resizing
                    var height = $('.console[data-id="442"] .lSPager>li img').innerHeight();
                    $('.console[data-id="442"] .pagerContainer button').height(height+'px');
                }
            
            function initNav442() {
                initNavDesktop442();
                initNavMobile442();

                $('.console[data-id="442"]')
                    .on('click', 'button.oe24lsSlide.previous', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        slider.goToPrevSlide();
                    })
                    .on('click', 'button.oe24lsSlide.next', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        slider.goToNextSlide();
                    });
            }

            function initNavDesktop442(){
                $container = $('.console[data-id="442"] .lSSlideWrapper');
            
                var $buttonPrev = $("<button>", {"class": "oe24lsSlide previous"});
                var $buttonNext = $("<button>", {"class": "oe24lsSlide next"});
                    
                $buttonPrev.html('<svg class="oe24lsSlideIcon" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><path d="M 0,50 L 30,100 L 40,100 L 10,50  L 40,0 L 30,0 Z" class="arrow"></path></svg>');
                $buttonNext.html('<svg class="oe24lsSlideIcon" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><path d="M 0,50 L 30,100 L 40,100 L 10,50  L 40,0 L 30,0 Z" class="arrow" transform="translate(100, 100) rotate(180) "></path></svg>');

                $container.append($buttonPrev).append($buttonNext);
            
            }
            function initNavMobile442(){
                $container = $('.console[data-id="442"] .lSPager');
                $container.wrap('<div class="pagerContainer"></div>');

                $divContainer = $('.console[data-id="442"] .pagerContainer');

                var height = $('.console[data-id="442"] .lSPager>li img').innerHeight();
                
                var $buttonPrev = $('<button>', {'class': 'oe24lsSlide previous'});
                var $buttonNext = $('<button>', {'class': 'oe24lsSlide next'});
                $buttonPrev.height(height+'px');
                $buttonNext.height(height+'px');
                    
                $buttonPrev.html('<svg class="oe24lsSlideIcon" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><path d="M 0,50 L 30,100 L 40,100 L 10,50  L 40,0 L 30,0 Z" class="arrow"></path></svg>');
                $buttonNext.html('<svg class="oe24lsSlideIcon" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><path d="M 0,50 L 30,100 L 40,100 L 10,50  L 40,0 L 30,0 Z" class="arrow" transform="translate(100, 100) rotate(180) "></path></svg>');

                $divContainer.append($buttonPrev).append($buttonNext);
            }
            
        });
    })();

       <div class="weatherCardTextContainer">
        <h2 class="weatherCardShortText">
         Schneefall, im S sonnig, -2/5°
        </h2>
        <p class="weatherCardText">
         An der Alpennordseite, besonders in den Staulagen fällt noch zeitweise Schnee. Sonst ziehen meist nur ein paar Schnee- oder Regenschauer durch und die Sonne scheint etwas häufiger. Schneefallgrenze um 600m Seehöhe. Wetterbegünstigt ist der Süden, hier bleibt es überwiegend trocken und auch die Sonne scheint hier häufiger. Der Wind weht mäßig bis lebhaft, in der Tauernregion und am Alpenostrand auch kräftig aus Nordwest bis Nord. Tageshöchsttemperaturen 2 bis 8 Grad.
        </p>
        <p class="weatherCardTextShowMore pb-2">
         <button class="btn" type="button">
          <span class="weatherCardTextButtonMore">
           <span class="weatherCardTextButtonCaption">
            Mehr anzeigen
           </span>
           <span class="weatherCardTextButtonIcon icofont-rounded-down">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="weatherCardTextButtonLess">
           <span class="weatherCardTextButtonCaption">
            Weniger anzeigen
           </span>
           <span class="weatherCardTextButtonIcon icofont-rounded-up">
           </span>
          </span>
         </button>
        </p>
       </div>

      <script>
       ;(function() {

    var weatherCardText = document.querySelector('.weatherCardContainer .weatherCardText');
    if (null === weatherCardText) {
        return;
    }

    var button = document.querySelector('.weatherCardContainer .weatherCardTextShowMore button');
    if (null === button) {
        return;
    }

    var buttenCaptionMore = button.querySelector('.weatherCardTextButtonMore');
    var buttenCaptionLess = button.querySelector('.weatherCardTextButtonLess');

    button.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
        if (OE24.util.hasClass(weatherCardText, 'showMore')) {
            OE24.util.removeClass(weatherCardText, 'showMore');
            buttenCaptionMore.style.display = 'inline';
            buttenCaptionLess.style.display = 'none';
        } else {
            OE24.util.addClass(weatherCardText, 'showMore');
            buttenCaptionMore.style.display = 'none';
            buttenCaptionLess.style.display = 'inline';
        }
    });

})();
      </script>
      <script>
       ;(function() {

    "use strict";

    var weatherCard = document.querySelector('.weatherCard');
    var weatherCardMap = weatherCard.querySelector('svg');
    var svgPaths = weatherCardMap.querySelectorAll('path');

    var elementPlaces = weatherCard.querySelectorAll('.place');
    var elementPlaceIcons = weatherCard.querySelectorAll('.placeIcon');
    var elementPlacePlaces = weatherCard.querySelectorAll('.placePlace');
    var elementPlaceTemperture = weatherCard.querySelectorAll('.placeTemp');

    var domain = 'https://www.wetter.at';
    var classReadyValue = 'placeReady';
    var arr;

    function initPlaces(places, iconsPath) {

        for (var i = 0; i < places.length; i++) {

            elementPlaceIcons[i].src = iconsPath + '/icon_' + places[i].icon + '.png';
            elementPlaceIcons[i].title = places[i].iconText;

            elementPlacePlaces[i].innerHTML = places[i].name;
            elementPlaceTemperture[i].innerHTML = places[i].temp + '&deg;'; //'&#8451;';

            // Signalisieren, dass das Places-Element mit Daten befuellt ist
            OE24.util.addClass(elementPlaces[i], classReadyValue);

            // Den Link zur Seite auf wetter.at als Attribut in die Wetterkarte schreiben.
            // Die Reihenfolge in den JSON-Daten *MUSS* mit der Reihenfolge der Bundeslaender
            // im SVG uebereinstimmen!
            svgPaths[i].setAttribute('data-link', places[i].link);
        }

    }

    function initMap(places) {

        var link, svgPaths = weatherCardMap.querySelectorAll('path');

        for (var i = 0; i < svgPaths.length; i++) {
            svgPaths[i].addEventListener('click', function(event) {
                event.preventDefault();
                link = this.dataset.link;
                window.open(domain + link);
            });
        }
    }

    try {

        var places = JSON.parse(weatherCard.dataset.places);
        var iconsPath = weatherCard.dataset.iconsPath;

        initPlaces(places, iconsPath);
        initMap(places);

    } catch(e) {
        console.log(e.name, e.message, e.fileName, e.lineNumber);
    }

})();
      </script>

     <script>
      (function() {
        $(document).ready(function() {
        
            var slider = $('.region[data-id="205"] .bundeslandSlider').lightSlider({
                gallery:true,
                autoWidth:false,
                item:9,
                loop:true,
                slideMove:1,
                slideMargin:0,
                enableDrag:true,
                enableTouch:true,
                controls:false,
                pager:false,
                responsive : [
                    {
                        breakpoint:768,
                        settings: {
                            item:3,
                        }
                    }
                ],
                onBeforeSlide: function() {
                    iom.c(oewa_data,1);                    
                },
                onSliderLoad: function(){
                    initNav205();
                    $('.region[data-id="205"]').addClass('lsSliderLoaded');
                    startSlider205();
                }
            });

            function initNav205() {
                
                $('.region[data-id="205"]')
                    .on('click', 'button.oe24lsSlide.previous', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        slider.goToPrevSlide();
                    })
                    .on('click', 'button.oe24lsSlide.next', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        slider.goToNextSlide();
                    });
            }

            function startSlider205() {
                var regionItems = document.querySelectorAll('.region .regionItem');
                var ajaxLoader  = document.querySelector('.contentBox.bundeslandBox .ajaxLoader');
                var regionCurrentActive, regionClicked, httpRequest, url, request;
                var regionsConfig = JSON.parse('[{"caption":"Wien","className":"region-wien","image":"\/misc\/bane\/images\/bundesland\/png\/wien.png","url":"#0","pageCode":0,"name":"Wien","link":"\/oesterreich\/chronik\/wien","channelname":"wien"},{"caption":"N\u00f6","className":"region-niederoesterreich","image":"\/misc\/bane\/images\/bundesland\/png\/niederoesterreich.png","url":"#0","pageCode":1,"name":"Nieder\u00f6sterreich","link":"\/oesterreich\/chronik\/niederoesterreich","channelname":"niederoesterreich"},{"caption":"Bgld","className":"region-burgenland","image":"\/misc\/bane\/images\/bundesland\/png\/burgenland.png","url":"#0","pageCode":2,"name":"Burgenland","link":"\/oesterreich\/chronik\/burgenland","channelname":"burgenland"},{"caption":"O\u00f6","className":"region-oberoesterreich","image":"\/misc\/bane\/images\/bundesland\/png\/oberoesterreich.png","url":"#0","pageCode":3,"name":"Ober\u00f6sterreich","link":"\/oesterreich\/chronik\/oberoesterreich","channelname":"oberoesterreich"},{"caption":"Sbg","className":"region-salzburg","image":"\/misc\/bane\/images\/bundesland\/png\/salzburg.png","url":"#0","pageCode":4,"name":"Salzburg","link":"\/oesterreich\/chronik\/salzburg","channelname":"salzburg"},{"caption":"Stmk","className":"region-steiermark","image":"\/misc\/bane\/images\/bundesland\/png\/steiermark.png","url":"#0","pageCode":5,"name":"steiermark","link":"\/oesterreich\/chronik\/steiermark","channelname":"steiermark"},{"caption":"Tirol","className":"region-tirol","image":"\/misc\/bane\/images\/bundesland\/png\/tirol.png","url":"#0","pageCode":6,"name":"Tirol","link":"\/oesterreich\/chronik\/tirol","channelname":"tirol"},{"caption":"Ktn","className":"region-kaernten","image":"\/misc\/bane\/images\/bundesland\/png\/kaernten.png","url":"#0","pageCode":7,"name":"K\u00e4rnten","link":"\/oesterreich\/chronik\/kaernten","channelname":"kaernten"},{"caption":"Vlbg","className":"region-vorarlberg","image":"\/misc\/bane\/images\/bundesland\/png\/vorarlberg.png","url":"#0","pageCode":8,"name":"Vorarlberg","link":"\/oesterreich\/chronik\/vorarlberg","channelname":"vorarlberg"}]');
                var region2Load = 0;

                function updateStories(stories) {
                    var condition, boxStories = document.querySelectorAll('.contentBox.bundeslandBox .story');

                    for (var i = 0; i < stories.length; i++) {
                        condition =
                            stories[i].hasOwnProperty('imageUrl') &&
                            stories[i].hasOwnProperty('leadText') &&
                            stories[i].hasOwnProperty('preTitle') &&
                            stories[i].hasOwnProperty('title') &&
                            stories[i].hasOwnProperty('url');

                        if ( ! condition) {
                            break;
                        }

                        boxStories[i].href = stories[i].url;

                        image = boxStories[i].querySelector('.storyImage img');
                        if (null === image) { continue; }
                        image.src = stories[i].imageUrl;

                        preTitle = boxStories[i].querySelector('.preTitle');
                        if (null === preTitle) { continue; }
                        preTitle.innerHTML = stories[i].preTitle;

                        title = boxStories[i].querySelector('.title');
                        if (null === title) { continue; }
                        title.innerHTML = stories[i].title;

                        leadText = boxStories[i].querySelector('.leadText');
                        if (null === leadText) { continue; }
                        leadText.innerHTML = stories[i].leadText;
                    }

                    setTimeout(function() {
                        // a little delay
                        OE24.util.removeClass(ajaxLoader, 'loadingData');
                    }, 500);
                }

                function updateRegionList() {

                    $('.region .regionItem').removeClass('regionActive');

                    if (typeof regionClicked !== 'undefined') {
                        OE24.util.addClass(regionClicked, 'regionActive');
                        regionCurrentActive = regionClicked;
                    }
                }

                function updateLink() {
                    for(i in regionsConfig){
                        if (i == region2Load) {
                            var name = regionsConfig[i].name;
                            var link = regionsConfig[i].link;

                            var el = document.querySelector('.bundeslandBox .bundeslandBoxShowMore .btn');
                            if (el) {
                                el.href = link;
                                el.innerHTML = 'Mehr ' + name + ' News' + ' <span class="icofont-rounded-right"></span>';
                            }
                            break;
                        }

                    }
                }

                function processContents() {

                    var stories;

                    if (httpRequest.readyState === XMLHttpRequest.DONE) {
                        if (httpRequest.status === 200) {
                            stories = JSON.parse(httpRequest.responseText);
                            if (false === Array.isArray(stories)) {
                                return;
                            }
                            updateStories(stories);
                            updateRegionList();
                            updateLink();
                        } else {
                            console.log('There was a problem with the request.');
                        }
                    }
                }

                function makeRequest(url,id) {

                    OE24.util.addClass(ajaxLoader, 'loadingData');

                    httpRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();

                    if (!httpRequest) {
                        console.log('Giving up (Cannot create an XMLHTTP instance');
                        return false;
                    }

                    region2Load = id;

                    httpRequest.onreadystatechange = processContents;

                    httpRequest.open('POST', url);
                    httpRequest.send();
                }

                for (var i = 0; i < regionItems.length; i++) {
                    if (OE24.util.hasClass(regionItems[i], 'regionActive')) {
                        regionCurrentActive = regionItems[i];
                    }
                    regionItems[i].addEventListener('click', function(event) {
                        event.preventDefault();
                        regionClicked = this;
                        url = this.dataset.link;
                        id = this.dataset.id;
                        makeRequest(url,id);
                    });
                }
            }
        });
    })();
     </script>
     <section class="content col-md-12 col-lg-8">
      <div class="contentBox bundeslandBox" data-count-stories="4">

       (function() {
        $(document).ready(function() {
            
            var slider = null;
            function loadConsole429(){
                slider = $('.console[data-id="429"] .consoleStories').lightSlider({
                    gallery:true,
                    autoWidth:false,
                    item:1,
                    loop:true,
                    slideMove:1,
                    slideMargin:0,
                    enableDrag:true,
                    enableTouch:true,
                    controls:false,
                    currentPagerPosition: 'left',
                                            thumbItem:5,
                        pager:true,
                                                            responsive : [
                        {
                            breakpoint:900,
                            settings: {
                                thumbItem:3,
                            }
                        },
                        {
                            breakpoint:620,
                            settings: {
                                thumbItem:2,
                            }
                        }
                    ],
                    onBeforeSlide: function() {
                        iom.c(oewa_data,1);                                        
                    },
                    onAfterSlide: function(el) {
                        $('#consoleCounter429').html(el.getCurrentSlideCount() + '/10');    
                        el.getCurrentSlideCount();                       
                    },

                    onSliderLoad: function(){
                        handleThumbnails429();                        window.setTimeout(initNav429, 50);
                    }
                });
            }
            var stories429 = new Array();
                            stories429[0] = 'Surf-Star (22) von Blitz getroffen - tot';
                            stories429[1] = 'Krimi in Schlussphase: Tirol zittert sich in Meistergruppe';
                            stories429[2] = '5:3 - WAC feiert Tor-Spektakel gegen Austria';
                            stories429[3] = '3:3 - St. Pöltens Last-Minute-Tor raubt Hartberg Top-6-Platz';
                            stories429[4] = ''+'Herr Marko, hat Mercedes nur geblufft?'+'';
                            stories429[5] = 'Feller gewinnt letzten Herren-Slalom in Lenzerheide';
                            stories429[6] = 'FC Liverpool steht vor Kader-Umbruch im Sommer';
                            stories429[7] = 'ÖFB gibt gekürzten Kader bekannt';
                            stories429[8] = 'Mega-Handgeld: Alaba mit neuem Club einig';
                            stories429[9] = 'Protestaktion? Gut-Behrami bricht RTL sofort ab';
            
            function findElement429(){

                if($('.console[data-id="429"] .container.headline').is(":visible")){
                    loadConsole429();
                    return;
                }
                window.setTimeout(findElement429, 1000);
            }
            findElement429();

                            window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
                    setTimeout(handleThumbnails429, 200);
                });
                
                var oe24SetButtonHeight429 = setInterval(setButtonSize429, 500);
               
                function setButtonSize429(){
                    var height = $('.console[data-id="429"] .lSPager>li img').innerHeight();
                    if(height>0) {
                        $('.console[data-id="429"] .pagerContainer button').height(height+'px');
                        clearInterval(oe24SetButtonHeight429);
                    }
                }
                
                function handleThumbnails429(){
                    $('.console[data-id="429"] ul.lSPager li').each(function(i){
                        var id = (i+1);
                        // counter
                        var $divCounter = $("<div>", {"class": "storyCounter"});
                        $divCounter.html(id);

                        $(this).append($divCounter);

                        // text
                        var $divText = $("<div>", {"class": "storyCaption"});
                        var $nodeMarker = $("<span>", {"class": "storyMarker"});
                        var $nodeText = $("<span>", {"class": "title"});
                        $nodeText.html(stories429[i]);

                        $divText.append($nodeMarker);
                        $divText.append($nodeText);

                        $(this).append($divText);
                    });

                    // set height - importend for resizing
                    var height = $('.console[data-id="429"] .lSPager>li img').innerHeight();
                    $('.console[data-id="429"] .pagerContainer button').height(height+'px');
                }
            
            function initNav429() {
                initNavDesktop429();
                initNavMobile429();

                $('.console[data-id="429"]')
                    .on('click', 'button.oe24lsSlide.previous', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        slider.goToPrevSlide();
                    })
                    .on('click', 'button.oe24lsSlide.next', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        slider.goToNextSlide();
                    });
            }

            function initNavDesktop429(){
                $container = $('.console[data-id="429"] .lSSlideWrapper');
            
                var $buttonPrev = $("<button>", {"class": "oe24lsSlide previous"});
                var $buttonNext = $("<button>", {"class": "oe24lsSlide next"});
                    
                $buttonPrev.html('<svg class="oe24lsSlideIcon" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><path d="M 0,50 L 30,100 L 40,100 L 10,50  L 40,0 L 30,0 Z" class="arrow"></path></svg>');
                $buttonNext.html('<svg class="oe24lsSlideIcon" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><path d="M 0,50 L 30,100 L 40,100 L 10,50  L 40,0 L 30,0 Z" class="arrow" transform="translate(100, 100) rotate(180) "></path></svg>');

                $container.append($buttonPrev).append($buttonNext);
            
            }
            function initNavMobile429(){
                $container = $('.console[data-id="429"] .lSPager');
                $container.wrap('<div class="pagerContainer"></div>');

                $divContainer = $('.console[data-id="429"] .pagerContainer');

                var height = $('.console[data-id="429"] .lSPager>li img').innerHeight();
                
                var $buttonPrev = $('<button>', {'class': 'oe24lsSlide previous'});
                var $buttonNext = $('<button>', {'class': 'oe24lsSlide next'});
                $buttonPrev.height(height+'px');
                $buttonNext.height(height+'px');
                    
                $buttonPrev.html('<svg class="oe24lsSlideIcon" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><path d="M 0,50 L 30,100 L 40,100 L 10,50  L 40,0 L 30,0 Z" class="arrow"></path></svg>');
                $buttonNext.html('<svg class="oe24lsSlideIcon" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><path d="M 0,50 L 30,100 L 40,100 L 10,50  L 40,0 L 30,0 Z" class="arrow" transform="translate(100, 100) rotate(180) "></path></svg>');

                $divContainer.append($buttonPrev).append($buttonNext);
            }
            
        });
    })();
      </script>
      <section class="xlBox">
       <div class="container headline">

     <script>
      (function() {
        
        $(document).ready(function() {
            
            var slider = null;
            function loadSlider638(){
                slider = $('.horoskop[data-id="638"] .horoskopSlider').lightSlider({
                    gallery:true,
                    autoWidth:false,
                    item:12,
                    loop:true,
                    slideMove:1,
                    slideMargin:0,
                    enableDrag:true,
                    enableTouch:true,
                    controls:false,
                    pager:false,
                    responsive : [
                        {
                            breakpoint:767,
                            settings: {
                                item:5,
                            }                        
                        },
                        {
                            breakpoint:400,
                            settings: {
                                item:3,
                            }                        
                        }
                    ],
                    onBeforeSlide: function() {
                        iom.c(oewa_data,1);                    
                    },
                    onSliderLoad: function(){
                        initNav638();
                        $('.horoskop[data-id="638"]').addClass('lsSliderLoaded');
                    }
                });
            }

            function initNav638() {
                
                $('.horoskop[data-id="638"]')
                    .on('click', 'button.oe24lsSlide.previous', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        slider.goToPrevSlide();
                    })
                    .on('click', 'button.oe24lsSlide.next', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        slider.goToNextSlide();
                    });
            }

            function findElement638(){
                if($('.horoskop[data-id="638"] .horoskopSlider').is(":visible")){ 
                    loadSlider638();
                    return;
                }
                window.setTimeout(findElement638, 1000);
            }
            findElement638();
        
        });
    })();
     </script>

                .on('click', 'button.oe24lsSlide.previous', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();

                    e.preventDefault();
                    slider.goToNextSlide();
                });

                box.css('height','100%');
            }

            token: tp.pianoId.getToken()
        };

        });

        const _pianoLogout = tp.pianoId.logout;
        tp.pianoId.logout = function(callback) {
            _pianoLogout(function() {
                OE24.events.raise('auth.update', _getAuthInfo());
                tp.api.callApi('/access/list', {}, function (accessInfos)  {
                    OE24.events.raise('access.update', accessInfos.data);
                });

                    callback( _getAuthInfo());
                }

        });

    }]);

            e.setAttribute('src', '//static.chartbeat.com/js/chartbeat_video.js');
            document.body.appendChild(e);
        }
        var oldonload = window.onload;
        window.onload = (typeof window.onload != 'function')
            ? loadChartbeat
            : function() { oldonload(); loadChartbeat(); };
    })();
  </script>

  <script>
   ;(function(adition) {

    if (typeof adition === 'undefined' || typeof adition.srq === 'undefined') {
        return;
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------

    var overlay = document.querySelector('.newStoriesOverlay');

    if (typeof overlay === 'undefined') {
        return;
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------

    var options = JSON.parse(overlay.dataset.options);

    // -----------------------------------------------

    var buttonClose = overlay.querySelector('.newStoriesButtonClose a');
    var buttonLoad  = overlay.querySelector('.newStoriesButtonLoad a');

    // -----------------------------------------------

    buttonClose.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        removeClass(options.activeClass);
        startTimeOut();
    });

    buttonLoad.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        removeClass(options.activeClass);
        var href = this.getAttribute('href');
        window.location.href = href;
    });

    // -----------------------------------------------

    function addClass(cssClass) {
        var arr = overlay.className.split(" ");
        if (arr.indexOf(cssClass) == -1) {
            overlay.className += " " + cssClass;
        }
    }

    function removeClass(cssClass) {
        if (overlay.classList)
            overlay.classList.remove(cssClass);
        else {
            var reg = new RegExp('(\\s|^)' + cssClass + '(\\s|$)');
            overlay.className = overlay.className.replace(reg, '');
        }
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------

    function loadAdition() {
        adition = adition || {};
        adition.srq = adition.srq || [];

        adition.srq.push(function(api) {
            api.configureRenderSlot('newstory').setContentunitId(parseInt(options.aditionId));
            api.renderSlot(options.aditionName);
            api.load([options.aditionName]).completeRendering();
        });
    }

    function startTimeOut() {
        var timeoutId = setTimeout(function() {
            addClass(options.activeClass);
            loadAdition();
        }, options.timeOutTime);
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------

    startTimeOut();

})(adition);
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
